asked the Minister of Local Government and ProvincialCouncils,—

(a) Will he submit to this House, separately and indetail—

(i) the amounts of funds provided to theHanguranketha Pradeshiya Sabha by the CentralGovernment and the financial institutions duringthe period from 02.04.2004 to 31.12.2005;

(ii) the revenue earned by this Pradeshiya Sabhaduring the aforesaid period;

(iii) the number of projects carried out; and

(iv) the expenditure incurred on them?

(b) Will he state whether these projects were carriedout in accordance with the accepted rules andregulations?

(c) Will he inform this House—

(i) whether the officers of the said PradeshiyaSabha including the Chairman have obtainedmoney for their personal use in addition to theabove projects;

(ii) if so, the actions taken against the said Chairmanand the officers?

(d) If not, why?

asked the Minister of Local Government and ProvincialCouncils:

(a) Will he submit to this House, separately and indetail—

(i) the amounts of funds provided to the WalapanePradeshiya Sabha by the Central Governmentand the financial institutions during the periodfrom 02.04.2004 to 31.12.2005;

(ii) the revenue earned by this Pradeshiya Sabhaduring the aforesaid period;

(iii) the number of projects carried out; and

(iv) the expenditure incurred on them?

(b) Will he state whether these projects were carriedout in accordance with the accepted rules andregulations?

(c) Will he inform this House—

(i) whether the officers of the said PradeshiyaSabha including the Chairman have obtainedmoney for their personal use in addition to theabove projects;

(ii) if so, the actions taken against the said Chairmanand the officers?

(d) If not, why?

asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administrationand Deputy Minister of Defence,—

(a) Will he inform this House—

(i) the number of complaints received by theMirigama Police Station in Gampaha District onthe day of the Local Government Elections heldon 30.03.2006; and

(ii) separately, the time taken by the said policestation to take relevant action with regard toeach of such complaints?

(b) Will he state separately—

(i) out of the aforesaid complaints, the number ofthose referred to the courts and to the MediationBoard;

(ii) the reasons for such reference; and

(iii) as to what action has been taken in respect ofeach of the aforesaid complaints by 01.05.2006?

(c) Is he aware that complaints were recorded in theordinary complaints register at the instigation ofpowerful politicians of the area, despite there beinga separate book for recording election relatedcomplaints?

(d) Will he inform this House as to what measureswould be taken against the Officers in Charge ofpolice stations who inquired into the complaintsaccording to the needs of politicians, withoutconducting a fair investigation?

(e) If not, why?

asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administrationand Deputy Minister of Defence:

(a) Will he inform this House—

(i) the number of complaints received by theNittambuwa Police Station in Gampaha Districton the day of the Local Government Electionsheld on 30.03.2006; and

(ii) separately, the time taken by the said policestation to take relevant action with regard toeach of such complaints?

(b) Will he state separately—

(i) out of the aforesaid complaints, the number ofthose referred to the courts and to the MediationBoard;

(ii) the reasons for such reference; and

(iii) as to what action has been taken in respect ofeach of the aforesaid complaints by 01.05.2006?

(c) Is he aware that complaints were recorded in theordinary complaints register at the instigation ofpowerful politicians of the area, despite there beinga separate book for recording election relatedcomplaints?

(d) Will he inform this House as to what measureswould be taken against the Officers in Charge ofpolice stations who inquired into the complaintsaccording to the needs of politicians, withoutconducting a fair investigation?

(e) If not, why?

asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Administrationand Deputy Minister of Defence :

(a) Will he inform this House—

(i) the number of complaints received by theKiribathgoda Police Station in Gampaha Districton the day of the Local Government Electionsheld on 30.03.2006; and

(ii) separately, the time taken by the said policestation to take relevant action with regard toeach of such complaints?

(b) Will he state separately—

(i) out of the aforesaid complaints, the number ofthose referred to the courts and to the MediationBoard;

(ii) the reasons for such reference; and

(iii) as to what action has been taken in respect ofeach of the aforesaid complaints by 01.05.2006?

(c) Is he aware that complaints were recorded in theordinary complaints register at the instigation ofpowerful politicians of the area, despite there beinga separate book for recording election relatedcomplaints?

(d) Will he inform this House as to what measureswould be taken against the Officers in Charge ofpolice stations who inquired into the complaintsaccording to the needs of politicians, withoutconducting a fair investigation?

(e) If not, why?

asked the Minister of Education :

(a) Will he reveal to this House, whether the SriSumangala Vidyalaya, Panadura had been shifted tothe Wekada area, about one kilometre from itspresent location, after being affected by the Tsunamiin 2004?

(b) Is he aware that a sum of about Rs. 275 million hasbeen allocated under outright aid from Japan for theconstruction of the required buildings for thisschool in the Wekada area?

(c) Will he state—

(i) whether it is due to a government decision toallocate the land for a different purpose thatthere is a delay in commencing the workconcerned despite the signing of the agreementfor the construction of the buildings; and

(ii) if not so, the reasons for such delay?

(d) Will he admit that—

(i) due to this delay, the country is at the risk oflosing this grant of nearly Rs. 275 million extendedas an outright aid; and

(ii) compensation have to be paid to the contractoron account of violating the contract agreement?

(e) Will he state as to what measures be taken toprevent this danger and the losses?

(f) If not, why?

Mr. Ariyaratne HewageSecretary,Ministry of Education,Fax No : 2785162

DRAFT CABINET DECISION

Given below is an extract of Item 56(i) of the minutes of theCabinet Meeting held on 26.04.2006. These minutes are to beconfirmed at the next Cabinet meeting.

Item 56 (i)

Re-location of Sri Sumangala College, Panadura after theTsunami Disaster and reconstructing it with Rs. 330 million -document dated 21.03.2006 presented by the Chief Minister,

ÀåÚÈèï¾àºëÉ16851686

Western Province - (Cabinet decision dated 22.03.2006 on CP/06/Misc (026) refers) this was considered along with theobservations of the Ministers of Education and Railways andTransport and it was decided to -

(a) allocate an extent of 03 Ac.30 perches of the landbelonging to the SLTB (with the buildings thereon)identified in the sketch attached to the observations ofthe Minister of Education and agreed to by the Ministerof Railways and Transport at this mecting, to the Ministryof Education, for the purpose of the proposed newbuildings, etc. for Sri Sumanagala Boys School,Panadura, sponsored by the Japanese Government :

(b) put up a suitable building for the SLTB at the expenseof the Ministry of Education, in the remaining portionof the land, and

(c) allocate the building belonging to the UDA in the vicinity(idenlfied and agreed to by the Minister of UrbanDevelopment and water Supply at the Meeting) to theSLTB, on terms to be mtually agreed to by the partiesconcerned, for use during the interim period till thebuilding reforred to at (b) above is constructed.

It was also agreed that no further extent of this land will beallocated to the school instead, offorts will be made to find andextent of alternate land in or around Panadura for the SLTB, inlieu of the land now allocated to the school.

(Mrs.) G. HapangamaSgd. D. WijesingheAdditional SecretarySecretary to the Cabinet28th April 2006

asked the Minister of Re-settlement,—

(a) Will he state in detail—

(i) what the refugee camps and welfare centresestablished for victims of war and naturaldisasters are in Sri Lanka;

(ii) the number of families and family members livingin them;

(iii) when such refugee camps were opened up;

(iv) the contribution made by the government fortheir maintenance; and

(v) the steps taken by the government to resettlethem?

(b) Will he submit separately details of the employeesworking in them and monthly wages paid to them?

(c) Will he table a detailed report about the shortcomingsprevalent in these refugee camps and welfare centresand about the employees working in them?

(d) If not, why?

In page 45 of the ‘‘ MahindaChinthana ’’ under the heading ‘‘ Fertilizer ’’ it states, Iquote :

‘‘ I will make........ ’’

Who is this ‘‘ I ’’ ? It is not Hemakumara. It is His ExcellencyMahinda Rajapaksa.

‘‘ I will make arrangements to offer 50 Kg bags of all types ofinorganic Fertilizer at Rs. 350 to farmers in order to increase theagricultural and plantation productivity. ’’

CEYLON FERTILIZER CO.(Ministry of Agriculture)FAX: 930423,947763TELEPHONE: 948555Your Ref:Our Ref:

24th October, 2003

Hon. S. B. Dissanayake,Minister of Agriculture & Livestock,Govijana Mandiraya,Battaramulla.

Hon’ble Sir,

SUPPLY OF FERTILIZER TO BATTICALOA FARMERSCOMPANY

Ceylon Fertilizer Co. Ltd has planned to improve the marketingactivities through out the country. As part of this programmearrangements have been made to appoint dealers in the Northern &Eastern Provinces.

Batticaloa Farmers Company (People’s) Ltd., one of the Stockiestsappointed for Batticaloa District had a discussion with your good selfon 8th August, 2003 regarding the problems faced by the farmers inthe area. At this meeting your consent was given to issue fertilizer to thisCompany without a Bank Guarantee, although it is a requirement ofour Company.

According to the requirement of this Company, the value of thefertilizer they buy at a time would be approximately Rs. Five Million.

Therefore, we would like to keep your good self informed of the factthat we are supplying the requirement of the Batticaloa Farmers Company(Pvt) Ltd. without a Bank Guarantee being obtained.

Yours faithfully,Ceylon Fertilizer Co. Ltd.

Jagath PereaChairman

[Àì. Ãå. 11.50]

Subscription : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available forRs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to theSUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATION BUREAU, No. 32, Transworks House,Lotus Road, Colombo 1. The fee should reach him on or bvefore November 30 each year.Late application for subscriptions will not be accepted.
